322→\t\tfields := strings.Fields(line)\n   323→\t\tif len(fields) < 4 {\n   324→\t\t\tcontinue\n   325→\t\t}\n   326→\t\tip, _, err := net.ParseCIDR(fields[3])\n   327→\t\tif err != nil {\n   328→\t\t\tcontinue\n   329→\t\t}\n   330→\t\tif !ip.IsGlobalUnicast() {\n   331→\t\t\tcontinue\n   332→\t\t}\n   333→\t\tif ipv4 := ip.To4(); ipv4 != nil {\n   334→\t\t\tipv4Addrs = append(ipv4Addrs, ipv4.String())\n   335→\t\t} else {\n   336→\t\t\tipv6Addrs = append(ipv6Addrs, ip.String())\n   337→\t\t}\n   338→\t}\n   339→\treturn\n   340→}\n   341→\n   342→func (l *base) detectPlatform() {\n   343→\tif l.getServerInfo().Mode.IsOffline() {\n   344→\t\tl.setPlatform(models.Platform{Name: \"unknown\"})\n   345→\t\treturn\n   346→\t}\n   347→\tok, instanceID, err := l.detectRunningOnAws()\n   348→\tif err != nil {\n   349→\t\tl.setPlatform(models.Platform{Name: \"other\"})\n   350→\t\treturn\n   351→\t}\n   352→\tif ok {\n   353→\t\tl.setPlatform(models.Platform{\n   354→\t\t\tName:       \"aws\",\n   355→\t\t\tInstanceID: instanceID,\n   356→\t\t})\n   357→\t\treturn\n   358→\t}\n   359→\n   360→\t//TODO Azure, GCP...\n   361→\tl.setPlatform(models.Platform{Name: \"other\"})\n   362→\treturn\n   363→}\n   364→\n   365→var dsFingerPrintPrefix = \"AgentStatus.agentCertHash: \"\n   366→\n   367→func (l *base) detectDeepSecurity() (string, error) {\n   368→\t// only work root user\n   369→\tif l.getServerInfo().Mode.IsFastRoot() {\n   370→\t\tif r := l.exec(\"test -f /opt/ds_agent/dsa_query\", sudo); r.isSuccess() {\n   371→\t\t\tcmd := fmt.Sprintf(`/opt/ds_agent/dsa_query -c \"GetAgentStatus\" | grep %q`, dsFingerPrintPrefix)\n   372→\t\t\tr := l.exec(cmd, sudo)\n   373→\t\t\tif r.isSuccess() {\n   374→\t\t\t\tline := strings.TrimSpace(r.Stdout)\n   375→\t\t\t\treturn line[len(dsFingerPrintPrefix):], nil\n   376→\t\t\t}\n   377→\t\t\tl.warns = append(l.warns, xerrors.New(\"Fail to retrieve deepsecurity fingerprint\"))\n   378→\t\t}\n   379→\t}\n   380→\treturn \"\", xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to detect deepsecurity %s\", l.ServerInfo.ServerName)\n   381→}\n   382→\n   383→func (l *base) detectIPS() {\n   384→\tips := map[string]string{}\n   385→\tfingerprint, 392→\n   393→func (l *base) detectRunningOnAws() (ok bool, instanceID string, err error) {\n   394→\tif r := l.exec(\"type curl\", noSudo); r.isSuccess() {\n   395→\t\tcmd := \"curl --max-time 1 --noproxy 169.254.169.254 http://169.254.169.254/latest/meta-data/instance-id\"\n   396→\t\tr := l.exec(cmd, noSudo)\n   397→\t\tif r.isSuccess() {\n   398→\t\t\tid := strings.TrimSpace(r.Stdout)\n   399→\t\t\tif !l.isAwsInstanceID(id) {\n   400→\t\t\t\treturn false, \"\", nil\n   401→\t\t\t}\n   402→\t\t\treturn true, id, nil\n   403→\t\t}\n   404→\n   405→\t\tswitch r.ExitStatus {\n   406→\t\tcase 28, 7:\n   407→\t\t\t// Not running on AWS\n   408→\t\t\t//  7   Failed to connect to host.\n   409→\t\t\t// 28  operation timeout.\n   410→\t\t\treturn false, \"\", nil\n   411→\t\t}\n   412→\t}\n   413→\n   414→\tif r := l.exec(\"type wget\", noSudo); r.isSuccess() {\n   415→\t\tcmd := \"wget --tries=3 --timeout=1 --no-proxy -q -O - http://169.254.169.254/latest/meta-data/instance-id\"\n   416→\t\tr := l.exec(cmd, noSudo)\n   417→\t\tif r.isSuccess() {\n   418→\t\t\tid := strings.TrimSpace(r.Stdout)\n   419→\t\t\tif !l.isAwsInstanceID(id) {\n   420→\t\t\t\treturn false, \"\", nil\n   421→\t\t\t}\n   422→\t\t\treturn true, id, nil\n   423→\t\t}\n   424→\n   425→\t\tswitch r.ExitStatus {\n   426→\t\tcase 4, 8:\n   427→\t\t\t// Not running on AWS\n   428→\t\t\t// 4   Network failure\n   429→\t\t\t// 8   Server issued an error response.\n   430→\t\t\treturn false, \"\", nil\n   431→\t\t}\n   432→\t}\n   433→\treturn false, \"\", xerrors.Errorf(\n   434→\t\t\"Failed to curl or wget to AWS instance metadata on %s. container: %s\",\n   435→\t\tl.ServerInfo.ServerName, l.ServerInfo.Container.Name)\n   436→}\n   437→\n   438→// http://docs.aws.amazon.com/AWSEC2/latest/UserGuide/resource-ids.html\n   439→var awsInstanceIDPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`^i-[0-9a-f]+$`)\n   440→\n   441→func (l *base) isAwsInstanceID(str string) bool {\n   442→\treturn awsInstanceIDPattern.MatchString(str)\n   443→}\n   444→\n   445→func (l *base) convertToModel() models.ScanResult {\n   446→\tctype := 451→\t\tContainerID: l.ServerInfo.Container.ContainerID,\n   452→\t\tName:        l.ServerInfo.Container.Name,\n   453→\t\tImage:       l.ServerInfo.Container.Image,\n   454→\t\tType:        ctype,\n   455→\t}\n   456→\n   457→\terrs, warns := []string{}, []string{}\n   458→\tfor _, e := range l.errs {\n   459→\t\terrs = append(errs, fmt.Sprintf(\"%+v\", e))\n   460→\t}\n   461→\tfor _, w := range models.ScanResult{\n   473→\t\tJSONVersion:       models.JSONVersion,\n   474→\t\tServerName:        l.ServerInfo.ServerName,\n   475→\t\tScannedAt:         time.Now(),\n   476→\t\tScanMode:          l.ServerInfo.Mode.String(),\n   477→\t\tFamily:            l.Distro.Family,\n   478→\t\tRelease:           l.Distro.Release,\n   479→\t\tContainer:         container,\n   480→\t\tPlatform: 508→}\n   509→\n   510→const (\n   511→\tsystemd  = \"systemd\"\n   512→\tupstart  = \"upstart\"\n   513→\tsysVinit = \"init\"\n   514→)\n   515→\n   516→// https://unix.stackexchange.com/questions/196166/how-to-find-out-if-a-system-uses-sysv-upstart-or-systemd-initsystem\n   517→func (l *base) detectInitSystem() (string, error) {\n   518→\tvar f func(string) (string, error)\n   519→\tf = func(cmd string) (string, error) {\n   520→\t\tr := l.exec(cmd, sudo)\n   521→\t\tif !r.isSuccess() {\n   522→\t\t\treturn \"\", xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to stat %s: %s\", cmd, r)\n   523→\t\t}\n   524→\t\tscanner := bufio.NewScanner(strings.NewReader(r.Stdout))\n   525→\t\tscanner.Scan()\n   526→\t\tline := strings.TrimSpace(scanner.Text())\n   527→\t\tif strings.Contains(line, \"systemd\") {\n   528→\t\t\treturn systemd, nil\n   529→\t\t} else if strings.Contains(line, \"upstart\") {\n   530→\t\t\treturn upstart, nil\n   531→\t\t} else if strings.Contains(line, \"File: ‘/proc/1/exe’ -> ‘/sbin/init’\") ||\n   532→\t\t\tstrings.Contains(line, \"File: `/proc/1/exe' -> `/sbin/init'\") {\n   533→\t\t\treturn f(\"stat /sbin/init\")\n   534→\t\t} else if line == \"File: ‘/sbin/init’\" ||\n   535→\t\t\tline == \"File: `/sbin/init'\" {\n   536→\t\t\tr := l.exec(\"/sbin/init --version\", noSudo)\n   537→\t\t\tif r.isSuccess() {\n   538→\t\t\t\tif strings.Contains(r.Stdout, \"upstart\") {\n   539→\t\t\t\t\treturn upstart, nil\n   540→\t\t\t\t}\n   541→\t\t\t}\n   542→\t\t\treturn sysVinit, nil\n   543→\t\t}\n   544→\t\treturn \"\", xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to detect a init system: %s\", line)\n   545→\t}\n   546→\treturn f(\"stat /proc/1/exe\")\n   547→}\n   548→\n   549→func (l *base) detectServiceName(pid string) (string, error) {\n   550→\tcmd := fmt.Sprintf(\"systemctl status --quiet --no-pager %s\", pid)\n   551→\tr := l.exec(cmd, noSudo)\n   552→\tif !r.isSuccess() {\n   553→\t\treturn \"\", xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to stat %s: %s\", cmd, r)\n   554→\t}\n   555→\treturn l.parseSystemctlStatus(r.Stdout), nil\n   556→}\n   557→\n   558→func (l *base) parseSystemctlStatus(stdout string) string {\n   559→\tscanner := bufio.NewScanner(strings.NewReader(stdout))\n   560→\tscanner.Scan()\n   561→\tline := scanner.Text()\n   562→\tss := strings.Fields(line)\n   563→\tif len(ss) < 2 || strings.HasPrefix(line, \"Failed to get unit for PID\") {\n   564→\t\treturn \"\"\n   565→\t}\n   566→\treturn ss[1]\n   567→}\n   568→\n   569→// LibFile : library file content\n   570→type LibFile struct {\n   571→\tContents []byte\n   572→\tFilemode os.FileMode\n   573→}\n   574→\n   575→func (l *base) scanLibraries() (err error) {\n   576→\tif len(l.LibraryScanners) != 0 {\n   577→\t\treturn nil\n   578→\t}\n   579→\n   580→\t// library scan for servers need lockfiles\n   581→\tif len(l.ServerInfo.Lockfiles) == 0 && !l.ServerInfo.FindLock {\n   582→\t\treturn nil\n   583→\t}\n   584→\n   585→\tl.log.Info(\"Scanning Lockfile...\")\n   586→\n   587→\tlibFilemap := map[string]LibFile{}\n   588→\tdetectFiles := l.ServerInfo.Lockfiles\n   589→\n   590→\t// auto detect lockfile\n   591→\tif l.ServerInfo.FindLock {\n   592→\t\tfindopt := \"\"\n   593→\t\tfor filename := range models.LibraryMap {\n   594→\t\t\tfindopt += fmt.Sprintf(\"-name %q -o \", filename)\n   595→\t\t}\n   596→\n   597→\t\t// delete last \"-o \"\n   598→\t\t// find / -type f -and \\( -name \"package-lock.json\" -o -name \"yarn.lock\" ... \\) 2>&1 | grep -v \"find: \"\n   599→\t\tcmd := fmt.Sprintf(`find / -type f -and \\( ` + findopt[:len(findopt)-3] + ` \\) 2>&1 | grep -v \"find: \"`)\n   600→\t\tr := exec(l.ServerInfo, cmd, noSudo)\n   601→\t\tif r.ExitStatus != 0 && r.ExitStatus != 1 {\n   602→\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to find lock files\")\n   603→\t\t}\n   604→\t\tdetectFiles = append(detectFiles, strings.Split(r.Stdout, \"\\n\")...)\n   605→\t}\n   606→\n   607→\tfor _, path := range detectFiles {\n   608→\t\tif path == \"\" {\n   609→\t\t\tcontinue\n   610→\t\t}\n   611→\n   612→\t\tif path, err = filepath.Abs(path); err != nil {\n   613→\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to abs the lockfile. err: %w, filepath: %s\", err, path)\n   614→\t\t}\n   615→\n   616→\t\t// skip already exist\n   617→\t\tif _, ok := libFilemap[path]; ok {\n   618→\t\t\tcontinue\n   619→\t\t}\n   620→\n   621→\t\tvar f LibFile\n   622→\t\tswitch l.Distro.Family {\n   623→\t\tcase constant.ServerTypePseudo:\n   624→\t\t\tfileinfo, err := os.Stat(path)\n   625→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   626→\t\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to get target file info. err: %w, filepath: %s\", err, path)\n   627→\t\t\t}\n   628→\t\t\tf.Filemode = fileinfo.Mode().Perm()\n   629→\t\t\tf.Contents, err = os.ReadFile(path)\n   630→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   631→\t\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to read target file contents. err: %w, filepath: %s\", err, path)\n   632→\t\t\t}\n   633→\t\tdefault:\n   634→\t\t\tcmd := fmt.Sprintf(`stat -c \"%%a\" %s`, path)\n   635→\t\t\tr := exec(l.ServerInfo, cmd, noSudo)\n   636→\t\t\tif !r.isSuccess() {\n   637→\t\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to get target file permission: %s, filepath: %s\", r, path)\n   638→\t\t\t}\n   639→\t\t\tpermStr := fmt.Sprintf(\"0%s\", strings.ReplaceAll(r.Stdout, \"\\n\", \"\"))\n   640→\t\t\tperm, err := strconv.ParseUint(permStr, 8, 32)\n   641→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   642→\t\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to parse permission string. err: %w, permission string: %s\", err, permStr)\n   643→\t\t\t}\n   644→\t\t\tf.Filemode = os.FileMode(perm)\n   645→\n   646→\t\t\tcmd = fmt.Sprintf(\"cat %s\", path)\n   647→\t\t\tr = exec(l.ServerInfo, cmd, noSudo)\n   648→\t\t\tif !r.isSuccess() {\n   649→\t\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to get target file contents: %s, filepath: %s\", r, path)\n   650→\t\t\t}\n   651→\t\t\tf.Contents = []byte(r.Stdout)\n   652→\t\t}\n   653→\t\tlibFilemap[path] = f\n   654→\t}\n   655→\n   656→\tvar libraryScanners []models.LibraryScanner\n   657→\tif libraryScanners, err = AnalyzeLibraries(context.Background(), libFilemap, l.ServerInfo.Mode.IsOffline()); err != nil {\n   658→\t\treturn err\n   659→\t}\n   660→\tl.LibraryScanners = append(l.LibraryScanners, libraryScanners...)\n   661→\treturn nil\n   662→}\n   663→\n   664→// AnalyzeLibraries : detects libs defined in lockfile\n   665→func AnalyzeLibraries(ctx context.Context, libFilemap map[string]LibFile, isOffline bool) (libraryScanners []models.LibraryScanner, err error) {\n   666→\tdisabledAnalyzers := []analyzer.Type{\n   667→\t\tanalyzer.TypeAlpine,\n   668→\t\tanalyzer.TypeAlma,\n   669→\t\tanalyzer.TypeAmazon,\n   670→\t\tanalyzer.TypeDebian,\n 677→\t\tanalyzer.TypeSUSE,\n   678→\t\tanalyzer.TypeUbuntu,\n   679→\t\tanalyzer.TypeApk,\n   680→\t\tanalyzer.TypeDpkg,\n   681→\t\tanalyzer.TypeRpm,\n   682→\t\tanalyzer.TypeApkCommand,\n   683→\t\tanalyzer.TypeYaml,\n   684→\t\tanalyzer.TypeTOML,\n   685→\t\tanalyzer.TypeJSON,\n   686→\t\tanalyzer.TypeDockerfile,\n   687→\t\tanalyzer.TypeHCL,\n   688→\t\tanalyzer.TypeSecret,\n   689→\t}\n   690→\tanal := analyzer.NewAnalyzerGroup(analyzer.GroupBuiltin, disabledAnalyzers)\n   691→\n   692→\tfor path, f := range libFilemap {\n   693→\t\tvar wg sync.WaitGroup\n   694→\t\tresult := new(analyzer.AnalysisResult)\n   695→\t\tif err := anal.AnalyzeFile(\n   696→\t\t\tctx,\n   697→\t\t\t&wg,\n   698→\t\t\tsemaphore.NewWeighted(1),\n   699→\t\t\tresult,\n   700→\t\t\t\"\",\n   701→\t\t\tpath,\n   702→\t\t\t&DummyFileInfo{size: int64(len(f.Contents)), filemode: f.Filemode},\n   703→\t\t\tfunc() (dio.ReadSeekCloserAt, error) { return dio.NopCloser(bytes.NewReader(f.Contents)), nil },\n   704→\t\t\tnil,\n   705→\t\t\tanalyzer.AnalysisOptions{Offline: isOffline},\n   706→\t\t); err != nil {\n   707→\t\t\treturn nil, 725→\n   726→// Name is\n   727→func (d *DummyFileInfo) Name() string { return \"dummy\" }\n   728→\n   729→// Size is\n   730→func (d *DummyFileInfo) Size() int64 { return d.size }\n   731→\n   732→// Mode is\n   733→func (d *DummyFileInfo) Mode() os.FileMode { return d.filemode }\n   734→\n   735→//ModTime is\n   736→func (d *DummyFileInfo) ModTime() time.Time { return time.Now() }\n   737→\n   738→// IsDir is\n   739→func (d *DummyFileInfo) IsDir() bool { return false }\n   740→\n   741→//Sys is\n   742→func (d *DummyFileInfo) Sys() interface{} { return nil }\n   743→\n   744→func (l *base) scanWordPress() error {\n   745→\tif l.ServerInfo.WordPress.IsZero() || l.ServerInfo.Type == constant.ServerTypePseudo {\n   746→\t\treturn nil\n   747→\t}\n   748→\tl.log.Info(\"Scanning 919→\tl.log.Info(\"Using Port Scanner: Vuls built-in Scanner\")\n   920→\n   921→\tlistenIPPorts := []string{}\n   922→\n   923→\tfor ip, ports := range scanDestIPPorts {\n   924→\t\tif nativeScanPort(scanDest string) (bool, error) {\n   945→\tconn, err := net.DialTimeout(\"tcp\", scanDest, time.Duration(1)*time.Second)\n   946→\tif err != nil {\n   947→\t\tif 956→\tconn.Close()\n   957→\n   958→\treturn true, nil\n   959→}\n   960→\n   961→func (l *base) execExternalPortScan(scanDestIPPorts map[string][]string) ([]string, error) {\n   962→\tportScanConf :=  1039→func formatNmapOptionsToString(conf *config.PortScanConf) string {\n  1040→\tcmd := []string{conf.ScannerBinPath}\n  1041→\tif len(conf.ScanTechniques) != 0 {\n  1042→\t\tfor _, technique := 1057→\n  1058→func (l *base) setScanTechniques() (func(*nmap.Scanner), error) {\n  1059→\tscanTechniques := l.getServerInfo().PortScan.GetScanTechniques()\n  1060→\n  1061→\tif len(scanTechniques) == err, path)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// skip already exist\n\t\tif _, ok := libFilemap[path]; ok {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar f LibFile\n\t\tswitch l.Distro.Family {\n\t\tcase constant.ServerTypePseudo:\n\t\t\tfileinfo, err := os.Stat(path)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to get target file info. err: %w, filepath: %s\", err, path)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tf.Filemode = fileinfo.Mode().Perm()\n\t\t\tf.Contents, err = os.ReadFile(path)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to read target file contents. err: %w, filepath: %s\", err, path)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tcmd := fmt.Sprintf(`stat -c \"%%a\" %s`, path)\n\t\t\tr := exec(l.ServerInfo, cmd, noSudo)\n\t\t\tif !r.isSuccess() {\n\t\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to get target file permission: %s, filepath: %s\", r, path)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tpermStr := fmt.Sprintf(\"0%s\", strings.ReplaceAll(r.Stdout, \"\\n\", \"\"))\n\t\t\tperm, err := strconv.ParseUint(permStr, 8, 32)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to parse permission string. err: %w, permission string: %s\", err, permStr)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tf.Filemode = os.FileMode(perm)\n\n\t\t\tcmd = fmt.Sprintf(\"cat %s\", path)\n\t\t\tr = exec(l.ServerInfo, cmd, noSudo)\n\t\t\tif !r.isSuccess() {\n\t\t\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to get target file contents: %s, filepath: %s\", r, path)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tf.Contents = []byte(r.Stdout)\n\t\t}\n\t\tlibFilemap[path] = f\n\t}\n\n\tvar libraryScanners []models.LibraryScanner\n\tif libraryScanners, err = AnalyzeLibraries(context.Background(), libFilemap, l.ServerInfo.Mode.IsOffline()); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\tl.LibraryScanners = append(l.LibraryScanners, libraryScanners...)\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// AnalyzeLibraries : detects libs defined in lockfile\nfunc AnalyzeLibraries(ctx context.Context, libFilemap map[string]LibFile, isOffline bool) (libraryScanners []models.LibraryScanner, err error) {\n\tdisabledAnalyzers := []analyzer.Type{\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeAlpine,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeAlma,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeAmazon,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeDebian,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypePhoton,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeCentOS,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeFedora,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeOracle,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeRedHatBase,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeRocky,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeSUSE,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeUbuntu,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeApk,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeDpkg,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeRpm,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeApkCommand,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeYaml,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeTOML,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeJSON,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeDockerfile,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeHCL,\n\t\tanalyzer.TypeSecret,\n\t}\n\tanal := analyzer.NewAnalyzerGroup(analyzer.GroupBuiltin, disabledAnalyzers)\n\n\tfor path, f := range libFilemap {\n\t\tvar wg sync.WaitGroup\n\t\tresult := new(analyzer.AnalysisResult)\n\t\tif err := anal.AnalyzeFile(\n\t\t\tctx,\n\t\t\t&wg,\n\t\t\tsemaphore.NewWeighted(1),\n\t\t\tresult,\n\t\t\t\"\",\n\t\t\tpath,\n\t\t\t&DummyFileInfo{size: int64(len(f.Contents)), filemode: f.Filemode},\n\t\t\tfunc() (dio.ReadSeekCloserAt, error) { return dio.NopCloser(bytes.NewReader(f.Contents)), nil },\n\t\t\tnil,\n\t\t\tanalyzer.AnalysisOptions{Offline: isOffline},\n\t\t); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to get libs. err: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\twg.Wait()\n\n\t\tlibscan, err := convertLibWithScanner(result.Applications)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to convert libs. err: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tlibraryScanners = append(libraryScanners, libscan...)\n\t}\n\treturn libraryScanners, nil\n}\n\n// DummyFileInfo is a dummy struct for libscan\ntype DummyFileInfo struct {\n\tsize     int64\n\tfilemode os.FileMode\n}\n\n// Name is\nfunc (d *DummyFileInfo) Name() string { return \"dummy\" }\n\n// Size is\nfunc (d *DummyFileInfo) Size() int64 { return d.size }\n\n// Mode is\nfunc (d *DummyFileInfo) Mode() os.FileMode { return d.filemode }\n\n//ModTime is\nfunc (d *DummyFileInfo) ModTime() time.Time { return time.Now() }\n\n// IsDir is\nfunc (d *DummyFileInfo) IsDir() bool { return false }\n\n//Sys is\nfunc (d *DummyFileInfo) Sys() interface{} { return nil }\n\nfunc (l *base) scanWordPress() error {\n\tif l.ServerInfo.WordPress.IsZero() || l.ServerInfo.Type == constant.ServerTypePseudo {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\tl.log.Info(\"Scanning WordPress...\")\n\tcmd := fmt.Sprintf(\"sudo -u %s -i -- %s core version --path=%s --allow-root\",\n\t\tl.ServerInfo.WordPress.OSUser,\n\t\tl.ServerInfo.WordPress.CmdPath,\n\t\tl.ServerInfo.WordPress.DocRoot)\n\tif r := exec(l.ServerInfo, cmd, noSudo); !r.isSuccess() {\n\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to exec `%s`. Check the OS user, command path of wp-cli, DocRoot and permission: %#v\", cmd, l.ServerInfo.WordPress)\n\t}\n\n\twp, err := l.detectWordPress()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed themes...)\n\tpkgs = append(pkgs, plugins...)\n\treturn &pkgs, nil\n}\n\nfunc (l *base) detectWpCore() (string, error) {\n\tcmd := fmt.Sprintf(\"sudo -u %s -i -- %s core version --path=%s --allow-root 2>/dev/null\",\n\t\tl.ServerInfo.WordPress.OSUser,\n\t\tl.ServerInfo.WordPress.CmdPath,\n\t\tl.ServerInfo.WordPress.DocRoot)\n\n\tr := exec(l.ServerInfo, cmd, noSudo)\n\tif !r.isSuccess() detectWpPlugins() ([]models.WpPackage, error) {\n\tcmd := fmt.Sprintf(\"sudo -u %s -i -- %s plugin list --path=%s --format=json --allow-root 2>/dev/null\",\n\t\tl.ServerInfo.WordPress.OSUser,\n\t\tl.ServerInfo.WordPress.CmdPath,\n\t\tl.ServerInfo.WordPress.DocRoot)\n\n\tvar plugins []models.WpPackage\n\tr := exec(l.ServerInfo, cmd, err\n\t}\n\tfor i := range plugins {\n\t\tplugins[i].Type = models.WPPlugin\n\t}\n\treturn plugins, nil\n}\n\nfunc (l *base) scanPorts() (err error) {\n\tl.log.Info(\"Scanning listen port...\")\n\tdest := l.detectScanDest()\n\topen, err := l.execPortsScan(dest)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\tl.updatePortStatus(open)\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc (l *base) detectScanDest() map[string][]string {\n\tscanIPPortsMap := map[string][]string{}\n\n\tfor _, p := range l.osPackages.Packages {\n\t\tif p.AffectedProcs == nil {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tfor _, proc := range p.AffectedProcs {\n\t\t\tif proc.ListenPortStats == nil {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfor _, port := range proc.ListenPortStats {\n\t\t\t\tscanIPPortsMap[port.BindAddress] = append(scanIPPortsMap[port.BindAddress], port.Port)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tscanDestIPPorts := map[string][]string{}\n\tfor addr, ports := range scanIPPortsMap {\n\t\tif addr == \"*\" {\n\t\t\tfor _, addr := range l.ServerInfo.IPv4Addrs {\n\t\t\t\tscanDestIPPorts[addr] = append(scanDestIPPorts[addr], ports...)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tscanDestIPPorts[addr] = append(scanDestIPPorts[addr], ports...)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tuniqScanDestIPPorts := map[string][]string{}\n\tfor i, scanDest := range scanDestIPPorts {\n\t\tm := map[string]bool{}\n\t\tfor _, e := range scanDest {\n\t\t\tif !m[e] {\n\t\t\t\tm[e] = true\n\t\t\t\tuniqScanDestIPPorts[i] = append(uniqScanDestIPPorts[i], e)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn uniqScanDestIPPorts\n}\n\nfunc (l *base) execPortsScan(scanDestIPPorts map[string][]string) ([]string, error) {\n\tif l.getServerInfo().PortScan.IsUseExternalScanner {\n\t\tlistenIPPorts, err := l.execExternalPortScan(scanDestIPPorts)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn []string{}, err\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn listenIPPorts, nil\n\t}\n\n\tlistenIPPorts, err := l.execNativePortScan(scanDestIPPorts)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn []string{}, err\n\t}\n\n\treturn listenIPPorts, nil\n}\n\nfunc (l *base) execNativePortScan(scanDestIPPorts map[string][]string) ([]string, error) {\n\tl.log.Info(\"Using Port Scanner: Vuls built-in Scanner\")\n\n\tlistenIPPorts := []string{}\n\n\tfor ip, ports := range scanDestIPPorts {\n\t\tif !isLocalExec(l.ServerInfo.Port, l.ServerInfo.Host) && net.ParseIP(ip).IsLoopback() {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor _, port := range ports {\n\t\t\tscanDest := ip + \":\" + port\n\t\t\tisOpen, err := nativeScanPort(scanDest)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn []string{}, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif isOpen {\n\t\t\t\tlistenIPPorts = append(listenIPPorts, scanDest)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn listenIPPorts, nil\n}\n\nfunc nativeScanPort(scanDest string) (bool, error) {\n\tconn, err := net.DialTimeout(\"tcp\", scanDest, time.Duration(1)*time.Second)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tif strings.Contains(err.Error(), \"i/o timeout\") || strings.Contains(err.Error(), \"connection refused\") {\n\t\t\treturn false, nil\n\t\t}\n\t\tif strings.Contains(err.Error(), \"too many open files\") {\n\t\t\ttime.Sleep(time.Duration(1) * time.Second)\n\t\t\treturn nativeScanPort(scanDest)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn false, err\n\t}\n\tconn.Close()\n\n\treturn true, nil\n}\n\nfunc (l *base) execExternalPortScan(scanDestIPPorts map[string][]string) ([]string, error) {\n\tportScanConf := l.getServerInfo().PortScan\n\tl.log.Infof(\"Using Port Scanner: External Scanner(PATH: %s)\", portScanConf.ScannerBinPath)\n\tl.log.Infof(\"External Scanner Apply Options: Scan Techniques: %s, HasPrivileged: %t, Source Port: %s\",\n\t\tstrings.Join(portScanConf.ScanTechniques, \",\"), portScanConf.HasPrivileged, portScanConf.SourcePort)\n\tbaseCmd := formatNmapOptionsToString(portScanConf)\n\n\tlistenIPPorts := []string{}\n\n\tfor ip, ports := range scanDestIPPorts {\n\t\tif !isLocalExec(l.ServerInfo.Port, l.ServerInfo.Host) && net.ParseIP(ip).IsLoopback() {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t_, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 5*time.Minute)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\n\t\tscanner, err := nmap.NewScanner(nmap.WithBinaryPath(portScanConf.ScannerBinPath))\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn []string{}, xerrors.Errorf(\"unable to create nmap scanner: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tscanTechnique, err := l.setScanTechniques()\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn []string{}, err\n\t\t}\n\t\tscanner.AddOptions(scanTechnique)\n\n\t\tif portScanConf.HasPrivileged {\n\t\t\tscanner.AddOptions(nmap.WithPrivileged())\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tscanner.AddOptions(nmap.WithUnprivileged())\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif portScanConf.SourcePort != \"\" {\n\t\t\tport, err := strconv.ParseUint(portScanConf.SourcePort, 10, 16)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn []string{}, xerrors.Errorf(\"failed to strconv.ParseUint(%s, 10, 16) = %w\", portScanConf.SourcePort, err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tscanner.AddOptions(nmap.WithSourcePort(uint16(port)))\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tcmd := []string{baseCmd}\n\t\tif strings.Contains(ip, \":\") {\n\t\t\tscanner.AddOptions(nmap.WithTargets(ip[1:len(ip)-1]), nmap.WithPorts(ports...), nmap.WithIPv6Scanning())\n\t\t\tcmd = append(cmd, \"-p\", strings.Join(ports, \",\"), ip[1:len(ip)-1])\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tscanner.AddOptions(nmap.WithTargets(ip), nmap.WithPorts(ports...))\n\t\t\tcmd = append(cmd, \"-p\", strings.Join(ports, \",\"), ip)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tl.log.Debugf(\"Executing... %s\", strings.Replace(strings.Join(cmd, \" \"), \"\\n\", \"\", -1))\n\t\tresult, warnings, err := scanner.Run()\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn []string{}, xerrors.Errorf(\"unable to run nmap scan: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif warnings != nil {\n\t\t\tl.log.Warnf(\"nmap scan warnings: %s\", warnings)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor _, host := range result.Hosts {\n\t\t\tif len(host.Ports) == 0 || len(host.Addresses) == 0 {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tfor _, port := range host.Ports {\n\t\t\t\tif strings.Contains(string(port.Status()), string(nmap.Open)) {\n\t\t\t\t\tscanDest := fmt.Sprintf(\"%s:%d\", ip, port.ID)\n\t\t\t\t\tlistenIPPorts = append(listenIPPorts, scanDest)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn listenIPPorts, nil\n}\n\nfunc formatNmapOptionsToString(conf *config.PortScanConf) string {\n\tcmd := []string{conf.ScannerBinPath}\n\tif len(conf.ScanTechniques) != 0 {\n\t\tfor _, technique := range conf.ScanTechniques {\n\t\t\tcmd = append(cmd, \"-\"+technique)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif conf.SourcePort != \"\" {\n\t\tcmd = append(cmd, \"--source-port \"+conf.SourcePort)\n\t}\n\n\tif conf.HasPrivileged {\n\t\tcmd = append(cmd, \"--privileged\")\n\t}\n\n\treturn strings.Join(cmd, \" \")\n}\n\nfunc (l *base) setScanTechniques() (func(*nmap.Scanner), error) {\n\tscanTechniques := l.getServerInfo().PortScan.GetScanTechniques()\n\n\tif len(scanTechniques) == 0 {\n\t\tif l.getServerInfo().PortScan.HasPrivileged {\n\t\t\treturn nmap.WithSYNScan(), nil\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn nmap.WithConnectScan(), nil\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, technique := range scanTechniques {\n\t\tswitch technique {\n\t\tcase config.TCPSYN:\n\t\t\treturn nmap.WithSYNScan(), nil\n\t\tcase config.TCPConnect:\n\t\t\treturn nmap.WithConnectScan(), nil\n\t\tcase config.TCPACK:\n\t\t\treturn nmap.WithACKScan(), nil\n\t\tcase config.TCPWindow:\n\t\t\treturn nmap.WithWindowScan(), nil\n\t\tcase config.TCPMaimon:\n\t\t\treturn nmap.WithMaimonScan(), nil\n\t\tcase config.TCPNull:\n\t\t\treturn nmap.WithTCPNullScan(), nil\n\t\tcase config.TCPFIN:\n\t\t\treturn nmap.WithTCPFINScan(), nil\n\t\tcase config.TCPXmas:\n\t\t\treturn nmap.WithTCPXmasScan(), nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil, xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to setScanTechniques. There is an unsupported option in ScanTechniques.\")\n}\n\nfunc (l *base) updatePortStatus(listenIPPorts []string) {\n\tfor name, p := range l.osPackages.Packages {\n\t\tif p.AffectedProcs == nil {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tfor i, proc := range p.AffectedProcs {\n\t\t\tif proc.ListenPortStats == nil {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfor j, port := range proc.ListenPortStats {\n\t\t\t\tl.osPackages.Packages[name].AffectedProcs[i].ListenPortStats[j].PortReachableTo = l.findPortTestSuccessOn(listenIPPorts, port)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (l *base) findPortTestSuccessOn(listenIPPorts []string, searchListenPort models.PortStat) []string {\n\taddrs := []string{}\n\n\tfor _, ipPort := range listenIPPorts {\n\t\tipPort, err := models.NewPortStat(ipPort)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tl.log.Warnf(\"Failed to find: %+v\", err)\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tif searchListenPort.BindAddress == \"*\" {\n\t\t\tif searchListenPort.Port == ipPort.Port {\n\t\t\t\taddrs = append(addrs, ipPort.BindAddress)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else if searchListenPort.BindAddress == ipPort.BindAddress && searchListenPort.Port == ipPort.Port {\n\t\t\taddrs = append(addrs, ipPort.BindAddress)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn addrs\n}\n\nfunc (l *base) ps() (string, error) {\n\tcmd := `LANGUAGE=en_US.UTF-8 ps --no-headers --ppid 2 -p 2 --deselect -o pid,comm`\n\tr := l.exec(util.PrependProxyEnv(cmd), noSudo)\n\tif !r.isSuccess() {\n\t\treturn \"\", xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to SSH: %s\", r)\n\t}\n\treturn r.Stdout, nil\n}\n\nfunc (l *base) parsePs(stdout string) map[string]string {\n\tpidNames := map[string]string{}\n\tscanner := bufio.NewScanner(strings.NewReader(stdout))\n\tfor scanner.Scan() {\n\t\tline := strings.TrimSpace(scanner.Text())\n\t\tss := strings.Fields(line)\n\t\tif len(ss) < 2 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tpidNames[ss[0]] = ss[1]\n\t}\n\treturn pidNames\n}\n\nfunc (l *base) lsProcExe(pid string) (string, error) {\n\tcmd := fmt.Sprintf(\"ls -l /proc/%s/exe\", pid)\n\tr := l.exec(util.PrependProxyEnv(cmd), sudo)\n\tif !r.isSuccess() {\n\t\treturn \"\", xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to SSH: %s\", r)\n\t}\n\treturn r.Stdout, nil\n}\n\nfunc (l *base) parseLsProcExe(stdout string) (string, error) {\n\tss := strings.Fields(stdout)\n\tif len(ss) < 11 {\n\t\treturn \"\", xerrors.Errorf(\"Unknown format: %s\", stdout)\n\t}\n\treturn ss[10], nil\n}\n\nfunc (l *base) grepProcMap(pid string) (string, error) {\n\tcmd := fmt.Sprintf(`cat /proc/%s/maps 2>/dev/null | grep -v \" 00:00 \" | awk '{print $6}' | sort -n | uniq`, pid)\n\tr := l.exec(util.PrependProxyEnv(cmd), sudo)\n\tif !r.isSuccess() {\n\t\treturn \"\", xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to SSH: %s\", r)\n\t}\n\treturn r.Stdout, nil\n}\n\nfunc (l *base) parseGrepProcMap(stdout string) (soPaths []string) {\n\tscanner := bufio.NewScanner(strings.NewReader(stdout))\n\tfor scanner.Scan() {\n\t\tline := strings.TrimSpace(scanner.Text())\n\t\tline = strings.Split(line, \";\")[0]\n\t\tsoPaths = append(soPaths, line)\n\t}\n\treturn soPaths\n}\n\nfunc (l *base) lsOfListen() (string, error) {\n\tcmd := `lsof -i -P -n`\n\tr := l.exec(util.PrependProxyEnv(cmd), sudo)\n\tif !r.isSuccess() {\n\t\treturn \"\", xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to lsof: %s\", r)\n\t}\n\treturn r.Stdout, nil\n}\n\nfunc (l *base) parseLsOf(stdout string) map[string][]string {\n\tportPids := map[string][]string{}\n\tscanner := bufio.NewScanner(strings.NewReader(stdout))\n\tfor scanner.Scan() {\n\t\tline := scanner.Text()\n\t\tif !strings.Contains(line, \"LISTEN\") {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tss := strings.Fields(line)\n\t\tif len(ss) < 10 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tpid, ipPort := ss[1], ss[8]\n\t\tportPids[ipPort] = util.AppendIfMissing(portPids[ipPort], pid)\n\t}\n\treturn portPids\n}\n\nfunc (l *base) pkgPs(getOwnerPkgs func([]string) ([]string, error)) error {\n\tstdout, err := l.ps()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn xerrors.Errorf(\"Failed to pkgPs: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\tpidNames := l.parsePs(stdout)\n\tpidLoadedFiles := map[string][]string{}\n\tfor pid := range pidNames {\n\t\tstdout :=
